    <script>
            $( ".newsletter2" ).submit(function( event ) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var form = $('.newsletter2 form');
            e = $(this);
            url = form.attr( "action" );
            input = form.serialize();
            $('.newsletter2 .err_msg').addClass('hide');
            $('.newsletter2 #but_subscribe').attr('disabled','disabled');
            var posting = $.post( url, input );
            posting.done(function( data ) {
            var d = $.parseJSON( data );
            
            if( d.err ){
                    $('.newsletter2 .err_msg').removeClass('hide').text(d.err.email);
                    $('.newsletter2 #but_subscribe').removeAttr('disabled');
            }else if( d.done ){
                    //alert(123);
                    e.html('<h3>شكراً لك تم اشتراكك بنجاح</h3>');
                    document.cookie = 'box233=show';

                    //-----------
                    setTimeout(function(){ 
                        $('#mailbox-id').modal('hide');
                        }, 2000);

                    //alert(3456);
                }
            });
            
            return;
		});
        </script>
        
        
            <script>
	    function getCookie(cname) {
		    var name = cname + "=";
		    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
		    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
		    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
			    var c = ca[i];
			    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				    c = c.substring(1);
			    }
			    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
				    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			    }
		    }
		    return "";
	    }

	</script>

<script>
    $().ready(function () {
        //初始化城市导航省市联动
        initProvinceCity2("navProvince_index", null, "navCity_index", null, "http://www.bao315.com/area/area_open.html");

        $("#navCityOpen").click(function () {
            var $areaId = $("#city").val();
            if ($areaId != null && $areaId != undefined && $areaId > 0) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: 'http://www.bao315.com/area/areaInfo.html',
                    type: "GET",
                    data: {cityId: $areaId},
                    dataType: "json",
                    cache: false,
                    async: false,
                    success: function (data) {
                        if ($.isEmptyObject(data)) {
                            return;
                        }
                        if (data["isHot"] == 2 && data["isOpen"] == 1 && data["areaNumber"] != null && data["areaNumber"] != undefined) {
                            location.href = "http://" + data["areaNumber"] + ".bao315.com/";
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $('.left-flex ul li:nth-child(2)').hover(function () {
            $('.qr-code').show();
        }, function () {
            $('.qr-code').hide();
        });
        $('.left-flex ul li:nth-child(1)').hover(function () {
            $('.left-consultation').show();
        }, function () {
            $('.left-consultation').hide();
        });
        $('.left-flex ul li').eq(2).click(function () {
            $("html,body").animate({
                scrollTop: 0
            }, 200);
        });
        $('.index-06-width div').hover(function () {
            index = $(this).index();
            $(this).children('p').stop().slideDown();
        }, function () {
            $(this).children('p').stop().slideUp();
        });
        //tab切换
        $("#score").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").show();
            $("#hotlist").hide();
            $("#signinglist").hide();
            $("#score").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#score').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        $("#hot").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").hide();
            $("#hotlist").show();
            $("#signinglist").hide();
            $("#hot").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#hot').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        $("#signing").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").hide();
            $("#hotlist").hide();
            $("#signinglist").show();
            $("#signing").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#signing').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        //tab切换结束
        $('body').on('click', '.province-sele-option p', function () {
            $('#province').val($(this).attr('id')).change();
            $('#navCity1').html("选择城市");

        });
        $('body').on('click', '.city-sele-option-01 p', function () {
            $('#city').val($(this).attr('id')).change();

        });
        $('.city-list .wrap-a a').each((i, v) => {
            if ($(v).text().length > 4) {
                $(v).css({
                    'width': 'auto',
                    'margin-right': '40px'
                })
            } else {
                $(v).css('width', '120px')
            }
        })
    });
</script>
